styles_format__lYsGI styles_richText__JVzKB text-gray-600">Hey Product Hunt community! 👋 I’m Dmytro, founder and CEO of Stripo, the all-in-one email design platform. If you’ve ever found email creation frustrating, slow, or full of back-and-forth approvals, trust me—I’ve been there too.

That’s exactly why we rebuilt Stripo from the ground up, making it smarter, faster, and more collaborative than ever. Today, I’m thrilled to introduce our brand-new editor—built for teams, powered by AI, and designed for the future of email marketing to transform the way you create emails.

What’s new?

👥 Collaboration tools—No more ‘Final_final_v2’ chaos 
Ever wished designing emails felt more like working in Google Docs? Now it does! Edit emails in real time with your team, leave comments, assign roles, track version history, and collaborate effortlessly—because great emails shouldn’t be a solo mission.

🧠 AI Hub—Your email co-pilot 
Imagine an assistant that helps you generate subject lines, email copy, and entire structures in seconds—without losing your brand voice. With our AI Assistant, you get the best of both worlds: automation to speed up production, plus the ability to review, refine, and personalize every email before it goes out. AI gives you a head start, but you’re always in control.

⚡ More power, more flexibility
We kept everything you love about Stripo and leveled it up. In addition to older features and capabilities, you will also benefit from new ones, including a dark mode interface, single sign-on authentication, custom UI, and even more to create stunning, high-performing emails.

Why we built this?
Email marketing is evolving, and our mission is to shape its future. We saw teams struggling with slow processes, scattered feedback, and too much manual work. So we spent months testing, refining, and listening to our users to eliminate bottlenecks and make email creation fast and seamless. Whether you're a marketer, designer, or part of a large enterprise team, this update is built to help you work smarter, not harder.

🤔 What’s your biggest email challenge? 
We’d love to hear from you! What slows you down the most when creating emails? Drop a comment below, and let’s chat.
🚀 Try the new Stripo today! As a special thank you, use the promo code STRIPOPH to get the Basic plan free for 2 months!
